<div>Rearranging gives:</div>
<div><span class="math-block ">

<div>Solve above, we get <span class="math-inline ">

<details>

<div>Calculating the integral:</div>
<div><span class="math-block ">

<div>substitution back to <span class="math-inline ">
<mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="SVG"><svg style="vertical-align: -0.025ex" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="1.294ex" height="1.025ex" role="img" focusable="false" viewBox="0 -442 572 453"><g stroke="currentColor" fill="currentColor" stroke-width="0" transform="matrix(1 0 0 -1 0 0)"><g data-mml-node="math"><g data-mml-node="mi"><path data-c="78" d="M52 289Q59 331 106 386T222 442Q257 442 286 424T329 379Q371 442 430 442Q467 442 494 420T522 361Q522 332 508 314T481 292T458 288Q439 288 427 299T415 328Q415 374 465 391Q454 404 425 404Q412 404 406 402Q368 386 350 336Q290 115 290 78Q290 50 306 38T341 26Q378 26 414 59T463 140Q466 150 469 151T485 153H489Q504 153 504 145Q504 144 502 134Q486 77 440 33T333 -11Q263 -11 227 52Q186 -10 133 -10H127Q78 -10 57 16T35 71Q35 103 54 123T99 143Q142 143 142 101Q142 81 130 66T107 46T94 41L91 40Q91 39 97 36T113 29T132 26Q168 26 194 71Q203 87 217 139T245 247T261 313Q266 340 266 352Q266 380 251 392T217 404Q177 404 142 372T93 290Q91 281 88 280T72 278H58Q52 284 52 289Z"></path></g></g></g></svg></mjx-container></span> gives the final answer:</div>
<div><span class="math-block ">

<div>where <span class="math-inline ">
<mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="SVG"><svg style="vertical-align: -0.05ex" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="1.719ex" height="1.645ex" role="img" focusable="false" viewBox="0 -705 760 727"><g stroke="currentColor" fill="currentColor" stroke-width="0" transform="matrix(1 0 0 -1 0 0)"><g data-mml-node="math"><g data-mml-node="mi"><path data-c="43" d="M50 252Q50 367 117 473T286 641T490 704Q580 704 633 653Q642 643 648 636T656 626L657 623Q660 623 684 649Q691 655 699 663T715 679T725 690L740 705H746Q760 705 760 698Q760 694 728 561Q692 422 692 421Q690 416 687 415T669 413H653Q647 419 647 422Q647 423 648 429T650 449T651 481Q651 552 619 605T510 659Q484 659 454 652T382 628T299 572T226 479Q194 422 175 346T156 222Q156 108 232 58Q280 24 350 24Q441 24 512 92T606 240Q610 253 612 255T628 257Q648 257 648 248Q648 243 647 239Q618 132 523 55T319 -22Q206 -22 128 53T50 252Z"></path></g></g></g></svg></mjx-container></span> is the constant of integration.</div>
<hr style="border:1px solid red" >
</details>
<br>
<div>(b) <span class="math-inline ">
<mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="SVG"><svg style="vertical-align: -0.912ex" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="9.352ex" height="2.884ex" role="img" focusable="false" viewBox="0 -871.7 4133.7 <summary><span class="details-marker">&nbsp;</span><span style="color:green">Solutions</span></summary><hr style="border:1px solid red" >
<div>Use the reciprocal function rule, let <span class="math-inline ">
<mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="SVG"><svg style="vertical-align: -0.566ex" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="13.295ex" height="2.262ex" role="img" focusable="false" viewBox="0 -750 5876.5 <ol start="3">
<li>In this question you must show detailed reasoning<br>
Find the exact values of the following:<br>
(a) <span class="math-inline ">

Then</div>

<div>Therefore the exact value is</div>

<details>
<summary><span class="details-marker">&nbsp;</span><span style="color:blue">Hint</span></summary><hr style="border:1px solid red" >
<div>This can use reciprocal rule or substitution</div>
<hr style="border:1px solid red" >
</details>
<br>
<details>
<summary><span class="details-marker">&nbsp;</span><span style="color:green">Solutions</span></summary><hr style="border:1px solid red" >
use substitution method:
Let $u=\sin x+1$, so $du=\cos x\,dx$. When $x=0$, $u=1$; when $x=\tfrac{\pi}{2}$, $u=2$. Thus

<div>Therefore,</div>
<div><span class="math-block ">

Alternatively, we can write <span class="math-inline ">
<mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="SVG"><svg style="vertical-align: -0.186ex" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="9.502ex" height="1.692ex" role="img" focusable="false" viewBox="0 -666 4200 answer.</div>

<div>Therefore</div>

<div>Let <span class="math-inline ">

<div>Therefore</div>

<div>Therefore</div>

<div>Then work out the values of <span class="math-inline ">
<mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="SVG"><svg style="vertical-align: 0" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="1.697ex" height="1.62ex" role="img" focusable="false" viewBox="0 -716 750 716"><g stroke="currentColor" fill="currentColor" stroke-width="0" transform="matrix(1 0 0 -1 0 0)"><g data-mml-node="math"><g data-mml-node="mi"><path data-c="41" d="M208 74Q208 50 254 46Q272 46 272 35Q272 34 270 22Q267 8 264 4T251 0Q249 0 239 0T205 1T141 2Q70 2 50 0H42Q35 7 35 11Q37 38 48 46H62Q132 49 164 96Q170 102 345 401T523 704Q530 716 547 716H555H572Q578 707 578 706L606 383Q634 60 636 57Q641 46 701 46Q726 46 726 36Q726 34 723 22Q720 7 718 4T704 0Q701 0 690 0T651 1T578 2Q484 2 455 0H443Q437 6 437 9T439 27Q443 40 445 43L449 46H469Q523 49 533 63L521 213H283L249 155Q208 86 208 74ZM516 260Q516 271 504 416T490 562L463 519Q447 492 400 412L310 260L413 259Q516 259 516 260Z"></path></g></g></g></svg></mjx-container></span> and <span class="math-inline ">
<mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="SVG"><svg style="vertical-align: 0" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="1.717ex" height="1.545ex" role="img" focusable="false" viewBox="0 -683 759 683"><g stroke="currentColor" fill="currentColor" stroke-width="0" transform="matrix(1 0 0 -1 0 0)"><g data-mml-node="math"><g data-mml-node="mi"><path data-c="42" d="M231 637Q204 637 199 638T194 649Q194 676 205 682Q206 683 335 683Q594 683 608 681Q671 671 713 636T756 544Q756 480 698 429T565 360L555 357Q619 348 660 311T702 219Q702 146 630 78T453 1Q446 0 242 0Q42 0 39 2Q35 5 35 10Q35 17 37 24Q42 43 47 45Q51 46 62 46H68Q95 46 128 49Q142 52 147 61Q150 65 219 339T288 628Q288 635 231 637ZM649 544Q649 574 634 600T585 634Q578 636 493 637Q473 637 451 637T416 636H403Q388 635 384 626Q382 622 352 506Q352 503 351 500L320 374H401Q482 374 494 376Q554 386 601 434T649 544ZM595 229Q595 273 572 302T512 336Q506 337 429 337Q311 337 310 336Q310 334 293 263T258 122L240 52Q240 48 252 48T333 46Q422 46 429 47Q491 54 543 105T595 229Z"></path></g></g></g></svg></mjx-container></span>. Then integrate both parts (terms).</div>

<div>Equating coefficients yields the linear system</div>

<div>Subtracting the second equation from the first gives <span class="math-inline ">
<mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="SVG"><svg style="vertical-align: -0.186ex" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="7.605ex" height="1.805ex" role="img" focusable="false" viewBox="0 -716 3361.6 798"><g stroke="currentColor" fill="currentColor" stroke-width="0" transform="matrix(1 0 0 -1 0 0)"><g data-mml-node="math"><g data-mml-node="mo"><path data-c="2212" d="M84 237T84 250T98 270H679Q694 262 694 250T679 230H98Q84 237 84 250Z"></path></g><g data-mml-node="mi" transform="translate(778, 0)"><path data-c="41" d="M208 74Q208 50 254 46Q272 46 272 35Q272 34 270 22Q267 8 264 4T251 0Q249 0 239 0T205 1T141 2Q70 2 50 0H42Q35 7 35 11Q37 38 48 46H62Q132 49 164 96Q170 102 345 401T523 704Q530 716 547 716H555H572Q578 707 578 706L606 383Q634 60 636 57Q641 46 701 46Q726 46 726 36Q726 34 723 22Q720 7 718 4T704 0Q701 0 690 0T651 1T578 2Q484 2 455 0H443Q437 6 437 9T439 27Q443 40 445 43L449 46H469Q523 49 533 63L521 213H283L249 155Q208 86 208 74ZM516 260Q516 271 504 416T490 562L463 519Q447 492 400 412L310 260L413 259Q516 259 516 260Z"></path></g><g data-mml-node="mo" transform="translate(1805.8, 0)"><path data-c="3D" d="M56 347Q56 360 70 367H707Q722 359 722 347Q722 336 708 328L390 327H72Q56 332 56 347ZM56 153Q56 168 72 173H708Q722 163 722 153Q722 140 707 133H70Q56 140 56 153Z"></path></g><g data-mml-node="mn" transform="translate(2861.6, 0)"><path data-c="31" d="M213 578L200 573Q186 568 160 563T102 556H83V602H102Q149 604 189 617T245 641T273 663Q275 666 285 666Q294 666 302 660V361L303 61Q310 54 315 52T339 48T401 46H427V0H416Q395 3 257 3Q121 3 100 0H88V46H114Q136 46 152 46T177 47T193 50T201 52T207 57T213 61V578Z"></path></g></g></g></svg></mjx-container></span>, so <span class="math-inline ">
<mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="SVG"><svg style="vertical-align: -0.186ex" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="7.605ex" height="1.805ex" role="img" focusable="false" viewBox="0 -716 3361.6 798"><g stroke="currentColor" fill="currentColor" stroke-width="0" transform="matrix(1 0 0 -1 0 0)"><g data-mml-node="math"><g data-mml-node="mi"><path data-c="41" d="M208 74Q208 50 254 46Q272 46 272 35Q272 34 270 22Q267 8 264 4T251 0Q249 0 239 0T205 1T141 2Q70 2 50 0H42Q35 7 35 11Q37 38 48 46H62Q132 49 164 96Q170 102 345 401T523 704Q530 716 547 716H555H572Q578 707 578 706L606 383Q634 60 636 57Q641 46 701 46Q726 46 726 36Q726 34 723 22Q720 7 718 4T704 0Q701 0 690 0T651 1T578 2Q484 2 455 0H443Q437 6 437 9T439 27Q443 40 445 43L449 46H469Q523 49 533 63L521 213H283L249 155Q208 86 208 74ZM516 260Q516 271 504 416T490 562L463 519Q447 492 400 412L310 260L413 259Q516 259 516 260Z"></path></g><g data-mml-node="mo" transform="translate(1027.8, 0)"><path data-c="3D" d="M56 347Q56 360 70 367H707Q722 359 722 347Q722 336 708 328L390 327H72Q56 332 56 347ZM56 153Q56 168 72 173H708Q722 163 722 153Q722 140 707 133H70Q56 140 56 153Z"></path></g><g data-mml-node="mo" transform="translate(2083.6, 0)"><path data-c="2212" d="M84 237T84 250T98 270H679Q694 262 694 250T679 230H98Q84 237 84 250Z"></path></g><g data-mml-node="mn" transform="translate(2861.6, 0)"><path data-c="31" d="M213 578L200 573Q186 568 160 563T102 556H83V602H102Q149 604 189 617T245 641T273 663Q275 666 285 666Q294 666 302 660V361L303 61Q310 54 315 52T339 48T401 46H427V0H416Q395 3 257 3Q121 3 100 0H88V46H114Q136 46 152 46T177 47T193 50T201 52T207 57T213 61V578Z"></path></g></g></g></svg></mjx-container></span>. Then <span class="math-inline ">
<mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="SVG"><svg style="vertical-align: -0.186ex" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="14.476ex" height="1.805ex" role="img" focusable="false" viewBox="0 -716 6398.6 Thus</div>

<div>Now integrate termwise:</div>
